# uz/cx-corpora.xml.gz

(src)="427664"> Information security , sometimes shortened to InfoSec , is the practice of defending information from unauthorized access , use , disclosure , disruption , modification , perusal , inspection , recording or destruction .
(src)="427665"> It is a general term that can be used regardless of the form the data may take ( e.g. electronic , physical).[1 ]
(trg)="3"> Axborot xavfsizligini ta ' minlash , ba ' zan qisqartirilgan AX , amalda axborotni himoyalash , ruxsatsiz kirish , ishlatish ( foydalanish ) , oshkor etilishi oldini olish ( konfediansiallik ) , buzilish , o ' zgartirish , personal , tekshirish , yozish yoki yo ' q qilish .
(trg)="4"> Undan biror shaxslar doirasida foydalanish va o ' zgartirish kiritish huquqi nazarda tutulishi mumkin ( masalan , elektron , jismoniy ) . [ 1 ]

(src)="427765"> IT security Sometimes referred to as computer security , Information Technology security is information security applied to technology ( most often some form of computer system ) .
(src)="427766"> It is worthwhile to note that a computer does not necessarily mean a home desktop .
(src)="427767"> A computer is any device with a processor and some memory .
(src)="427768"> Such devices can range from non-networked standalone devices as simple as calculators , to networked mobile computing devices such as smartphones and tablet computers .
(src)="427769"> IT security specialists are almost always found in any major enterprise/establishment due to the nature and value of the data within larger businesses .
(src)="427770"> They are responsible for keeping all of the technology within the company secure from malicious cyber attacks that often attempt to breach into critical private information or gain control of the internal systems .
(src)="427771"> Information assurance The act of ensuring that data is not lost when critical issues arise .
(src)="427772"> These issues include , but are not limited to : natural disasters , computer/server malfunction , physical theft , or any other instance where data has the potential of being lost .
(src)="427773"> Since most information is stored on computers in our modern era , information assurance is typically dealt with by IT security specialists .
(src)="427774"> One of the most common methods of providing information assurance is to have an off-site backup of the data in case one of the mentioned issues arise .
(trg)="72"> ATda xavfsizlik Ba ' zan kompyuter xavfsizligi  atamasi sifatida ataladi .
(trg)="73"> Axborot Texnologiyasi xavfsizligi , axborot xavfsizligini tatbiq qilish texnologiyasi ( ko ' pincha kompyuter tizimi ) ni xavfsizligini ta ' minlash sifatida ishlatiladi .
(trg)="74"> U arzigulik uchun eslatma bu kompyuter emas , albatta degani bir bosh sahifa ish stoli .
(trg)="75"> Kompyuter har qanday qurilma bilan bir protsessor va ba ' zi bir xotira .
(trg)="76"> Bunday qurilmalar mumkin qator nodavlat tarmoq mustaqil qurilmalar kabi oddiy hisob , tarmoq mobil hisoblash asboblari kabi smartfonlar va planshet kompyuterlar uchun .
(trg)="77"> U xavfsizlik mutaxassislar bor deyarli har doim topilgan har qanday yirik korxona / o ' rnatilishi tufayli tabiat va qiymati ma ' lumotlar ichida katta biznes .
(trg)="78"> Ular uchun mas ' ul bo ' lgan tutib , barcha texnologiyasi , kompaniya ichida xavfsiz dan yomon kiber hujumlar , deb tez-tez harakat qilish buzilishi ichiga tanqidiy xususiy ma ' lumot yoki daromad nazorat qilish , ichki tizimlari .
(trg)="79"> Axborot kafolati Ish ta ' minlash ma ' lumotlarni emas , yo ' qolgan bo ' lsa , muhim masalalar yuzaga keladi .
(trg)="80"> Bu masalalarni o ' z ichiga oladi , lekin , cheklamagan holda : tabiiy ofatlar , kompyuter / server nosozligi , jismoniy o ' g ' irlik , yoki har qanday boshqa misol qaerda ma ' lumotlar salohiyatiga ega bo ' lish yo ' qolgan .
(trg)="81"> Beri eng axborot saqlanadi bo ' yicha kompyuterlar bizning zamonaviy davrda , axborot kafolati hisoblanadi , odatda , muomala bilan bilan U xavfsizlik mutaxassislar .
(trg)="82"> Biri eng keng tarqalgan usullari ma ' lumot taqdim etish kafolati hisoblanadi kerak , bir off-sayt zaxira ma ' lumotlar holda bir aytib o ' tilgan masalalar yuzaga keladi .
(src)="427779"> Since their introduction in 1992 , the FIFA World Rankings have been the matter of much debate , particularly regarding the calculation procedure and the resulting disparity between generally perceived quality and world ranking of some teams .
(src)="427780"> For example , Norway was ranked second in October 1993 and July–August 1995,[9 ] and the United States reached fourth in 2006 , to the surprise of even their own players.[10 ] However , criticism regarding the unrealistic ranking continued even after the introduction of the new formula .
(src)="427781"> Israel 's climb to 15th in November 2008 raised a few eyebrows even in the Israeli press,[11][12][13 ] with the team missing a huge opportunity to break into the top 10 after conceding a last gasp equaliser against Latvia.[14 ] Similarly , Belgium 's rank of world number 1 in November 2015 was met with skepticism in the press , given that Belgium had only played in one tournament in the past 13 years.[15 ]

(src)="428283"> ↑ Traditional names for the feast in English are " Easter Day " , as in the Book of Common Prayer , " Easter Sunday " , used by James Ussher ( The Whole Works of the Most Rev. James Ussher , Volume 4 ) and Samuel Pepys ( The Diary of Samuel Pepys , Volume 2 ) and plain " Easter " , as in books printed in 1575 , 1584 , 1586 ↑ In the Eastern Orthodox Church , the Greek word Pascha is used for the celebration ; in English , the analogous word is Pasch.[1][2 ] ↑ Preferred by some Protestants.[3][4 ] ↑ Old English pronunciation :  [ ˈæːɑstre , ˈeːostre ] ↑ Acts 2:1 ; 12:3 ; 20:6 ; 27:9 , 1  Cor 16:8 ↑ Eusebius reports that Dionysius , Bishop of Alexandria , proposed an 8-year Easter cycle , and quotes a letter from Anatolius , Bishop of Laodicea , that refers to a 19-year cycle.[62 ] An 8-year cycle has been found inscribed on a statue unearthed in Rome in the 17th century , and since dated to the 3rd century.[63 ]

(src)="428448"> Though before the final decades of the 2nd century only accessible as an exegetical tradition , already in the Pauline letters the Exodus saga is deeply involved with the celebration of bath and meal .
(src)="428449"> Even here , this relationship does not suddenly appear , but represents developments in ritual narrative that mus have begun at the very inception of the Christian message .
(src)="428450"> Jesus of Nazareth was crucified during Pesach-Mazzot , an event that a new covenant people of Jews and Gentiles both saw as definitive and defining .
(src)="428451"> Ex 12 is thus one of the few reliable guides for tracing the synergism among ritual , text , and kerygma before the Council of Nicaea . ↑ Sozomen , Book 7 , Chapter 18 ↑ The Date of Easter .

(src)="428554"> The early Christians of Mesopotamia had the custom of dyeing and decorating eggs at Easter .
(src)="428555"> They were stained red , in memory of the blood of Christ , shed at His crucifixion .
(src)="428556"> The Church adopted the custom , and regarded the eggs as the emblem of the resurrection , as is evinced by the benediction of Pope Paul V. , about 1610 , which reads thus : " Bless , O Lord ! we beseech thee , this thy creature of eggs , that it may become a wholesome sustenance to thy faithful servants , eating it in thankfulness to thee on account of the resurrection of the Lord . "

(trg)="644"> Easter eggs are used as a Christian symbol to represent the empty tomb .
(trg)="645"> The outside of the egg looks dead but inside there is new life , which is going to break out .
(trg)="646"> The Easter egg is a reminder that Jesus will rise from His tomb and bring new life .
(trg)="647"> Eastern Orthodox Christians dye boiled eggs red to represent the blood of Christ shed for the sins of the world .
(trg)="648"> 1 2 The Guardian , Volume 29 .
(trg)="649"> H. Harbaugh .
(trg)="650"> 1878 .

(trg)="652"> Just so , on that first Easter morning , Jesus came to life and walked out of the tomb , and left it , as it were , an empty shell .
(trg)="653"> Just so , too , when the Christian dies , the body is left in the grave , an empty shell , but the soul takes wings and flies away to be with God .
(trg)="654"> Thus you see that though an egg seems to be as dead as a sone , yet it really has life in it ; and also it is like Christ ' s dead body , which was raised to life again .
(trg)="655"> This is the reason we use eggs on Easter .

(trg)="749"> Though before the final decades of the 2nd century only accessible as an exegetical tradition , already in the Pauline letters the Exodus saga is deeply involved with the celebration of bath and meal .
(trg)="750"> Even here , this relationship does not suddenly appear , but represents developments in ritual narrative that mus have begun at the very inception of the Christian message .
(trg)="751"> Jesus of Nazareth was crucified during Pesach-Mazzot , an event that a new covenant people of Jews and Gentiles both saw as definitive and defining .
(trg)="752"> Ex 12 is thus one of the few reliable guides for tracing the synergism among ritual , text , and kerygma before the Council of Nicaea . ↑ Sozomen , Book 7 , Chapter 18 ↑ The Date of Easter .

(trg)="850"> The tradition of Easter eggs dates back to early Christians in Mesopotamia .
(trg)="851"> The Easter egg is a reminder that Jesus rose from the grave , promising an eternal life for believers . | access-date = requires | url = ( help ) ↑ Donahoe ' s Magazine , Volume 5 .
(trg)="852"> T.B. Noonan .
(trg)="853"> 1881 .
(trg)="854"> Retrieved 24 April 2014 .
(trg)="855"> The early Christians of Mesopotamia had the custom of dyeing and decorating eggs at Easter .
(trg)="856"> They were stained red , in memory of the blood of Christ , shed at His crucifixion .
(trg)="857"> The Church adopted the custom , and regarded the eggs as the emblem of the resurrection , as is evinced by the benediction of Pope Paul V. , about 1610 , which reads thus : " Bless , O Lord ! we beseech thee , this thy creature of eggs , that it may become a wholesome sustenance to thy faithful servants , eating it in thankfulness to thee on account of the resurrection of the Lord . "
(trg)="858"> Thus the custom has come down from ages lost in antiquity . ) ↑ " Easter Egg Roll " .

(src)="428560"> Uzbekistan ( US i/ʊz.ˈbɛk.ɪ.ˌstæn/ , UK /ʊz.ˌbɛk.ɪ.ˈstɑːn/ ) , officially the Republic of Uzbekistan ( Uzbek : Oʻzbekiston Respublikasi/Ўзбекистон Республикаси ) , is a doubly landlocked country in Central Asia .
(src)="428561"> It is a unitary , constitutional , presidential republic , comprising 12 provinces , 1 autonomous republic , and 1 capital city .
(src)="428562"> Uzbekistan is bordered by five countries : Kazakhstan to the north ; Tajikistan to the southeast ; Kyrgyzstan to the northeast ; Afghanistan to the south ; and Turkmenistan to the southwest .
(trg)="861"> O ' zbekiston ( AQSH men / ʊz.ˈbshtat ko ' pk.ɪ.ˌstæn / , Buyuk BRITANIYA / ʊz.ˌbshtat ko ' pk.ɪ.ˈstɑːn / ) , rasman , O ' zbekiston ( o ' zbek : O ' zbekiston Respublikasi / Ўзбекистон Республикаси ) , ikki karra quruqlikda joylashgan mamlakat ichida Markaziy Osiyo .
(trg)="862"> U bir unitar korxonasi , konstitutsiyaviy , o ' zbekiston respublikasi olgan 12 viloyatlari , 1 muxtor respublikasi va 1 poytaxt shahar .

(src)="428565"> Christopher Robert Evans ( born June 13 , 1981)[1 ] is an American actor .
(src)="428566"> Evans is best known for his superhero roles as the Marvel Comics characters Captain America in the Marvel Cinematic Universe and the Human Torch in Fantastic Four .
(src)="428567"> He began his career on the 2000 television series Opposite Sex , moving to film in 2001 with the teen comedy Not Another Teen Movie .
(src)="428568"> In 2013 , he starred as the lead in the critically acclaimed science fiction action film Snowpiercer , and in 2015 , he made his directorial debut with the drama Before We Go , in which he also starred .
(trg)="865"> Kristofer Robert Evans ( 1981-yilning 13-iyunida tug`ilgan) amerikalik superqahramonlar rollari ijrochisi.
(trg)="866"> U o`zining "Kapitan Amerika", "Fantastik to`rtlik" kabi kinolardagi rollari bilan mashhur.
(trg)="867"> U o`z karerasini 2000-yilda "Qaramaqarshilik" (Opposite sex) teleserialida boshlagan.
(trg)="868"> 2013-yildan boshlab u Janubiy Koreaning " Snowpiercer " ( ingilizcha ) filmida suratga tushib boshladi .
(trg)="869"> 2015-yilga kelib kino olamida ancha tetik bo`lib qolgan Kirs, o`zining rejissyorlik mahoratini "Ketishdan oldin" ("Before We Go") filmida sinab ko`rdi.

(trg)="871"> Yoshligi
(src)="428570"> Chris Evans was born in Boston[2 ] and raised in the town of Sudbury.[3 ] His mother , Lisa ( Capuano ) , is an artistic director at the Concord Youth Theater,[4][5 ] and his father , Robert Evans , is a dentist.[6 ] He has two sisters , Carly,[6 ] a graduate of New York University 's Tisch School of the Arts and a high school drama and English teacher at Lincoln-Sudbury Regional High School,[4][7 ] Shanna,[6 ] and a younger[8 ] brother , Scott,[6 ] who was featured on the ABC soap opera One Life to Live .
(src)="428571"> Their uncle , Mike Capuano , represents the same Massachusetts Congressional district formerly represented by Tip O'Neill.[9 ] His family has been in America since the colonial era.[10 ] His mother is of half Italian and half Irish ancestry.[9][11][12 ] He and his siblings were raised Catholic.[11][12 ]

(src)="428808"> Muhammad Yunus ( Bengali : মুহাম্মদ ইউনূস ; born 28 June 1940 ) is a Bangladeshi social entrepreneur , banker , economist , and civil society leader who was awarded the Nobel Peace Prize for founding the Grameen Bank and pioneering the concepts of microcredit and microfinance .
(src)="428809"> These loans are given to entrepreneurs too poor to qualify for traditional bank loans .
(src)="428810"> In 2006 , Yunus and the Grameen Bank were jointly awarded the Nobel Peace Prize " for their efforts through microcredit to create economic and social development from below " .
(src)="428811"> The Norwegian Nobel Committee said that " lasting peace cannot be achieved unless large population groups find ways in which to break out of poverty " and that " across cultures and civilizations , Yunus and Grameen Bank have shown that even the poorest of the poor can work to bring about their own development".[2 ] Yunus has received several other national and international honours .
(src)="428812"> He received the United States Presidential Medal of Freedom in 2009 and the Congressional Gold Medal in 2010.[3 ]
(trg)="1108"> Muhammad Yunus ( beng . - { মুহাম্মদ ইউনূস } - ; 1940-yil 28-iyun kuni tugʻilgan - [ [ bangladesh ] ] link  ijtimoiy tadbirkor , bankir , iqtisodchi va fuqarolik jamiyati rahbari .  Grameen Bankiga asos solgani hamda [ [ mikrokredit ] ] va [ [ mikrofinans ] ] tushunachalarini ilgari surgani uchun Nobel tinchlik mukofoti bilan taqdirlangan .
(trg)="1109"> Bunday kreditlar anʼanaviy bank kreditlari uchun oʻta kambagʻal hisoblangan tadbirkorlarga veriladi .  2006-yilda , Yunus va Grameen Banki birgalikda " mikrokredit yordamida ijtimoiy va iqtisodiy rivojlanishni tubdan boshlashga qaratiglan saʼy-harakatlari " uchun Tinchlik Nobel mukofotiga sazovor boʻldi .
(trg)="1110"> Norvegiya Nobel qoʻmitasi  " yirik aholi guruhlari qashshoqlikdan chiqish yoʻllarini topmasa doimiy tinchlik oʻrnatib boʻlmaydi " hamda „ Yunus va Grameen Banki eng kambagʻal kambagʻalalr ham oʻz rivojlanishlariga sababchi boʻla olishlari mumkinligini koʻrsatdi " , dedi [ 2 ] .  Yunus yana bir necha boshqa milliy va xalqaro sovrinlarni qoʻlga kiritgan .
(trg)="1111"> U 2009-yilda AQSH  Prezidenti erkinlik medali , 2010-yilda Kongress oltin medali bilan taqdirlandi . [ 3 ]
(src)="428813"> In 2008 , he was rated number 2 in Foreign Policy magazine 's list of the ' Top 100 Global Thinkers'.[4 ]
(trg)="1112"> 2008 yilda Yunus Foreign Policy jurnali tuzgan Yuz globall fikrlovchi roʻyxatida ikkinchi oʻringa qoʻyildi . [ 4 ]

(src)="429159"> Satellite craters
(trg)="1456"> Atrofidagi kraterlar
(src)="429160"> Al-Khwarizmi is a lunar impact crater located on the far side of the Moon .
(src)="429161"> It lies to the southeast of the crater Moiseev , and northeast of Saenger .
(trg)="1457"> Al-Xorazmiy krateri  [ [ Oy ] ] ning [ [ Yer ] ] ga teskari tomonida ,  Moiseev  kraterining janubi-sharqiy va  Saenger  kraterining shimoliy-sharqiy tomonida joylashgan .
(src)="429169"> Al-Khwarizmi Latitude Longitude Diameter B 9.0° N 107.4° E 62  km G 6.9° N 107.1° E 95  km H 6.0° N 109.2° E 50  km J 6.2° N 107.6° E 47  km K 4.6° N 107.6° E 26  km L 3.9° N 107.4° E 35  km M 3.1° N 107.0° E 18  km T 7.0° N 104.5° E 15  km
(trg)="1458"> Al-Xorazmiy Kenglik Uzunlik Diametr B 9.0 ° N 107.4 ° E 62 km G Hajmi-6,9 ° N 107.1 ° E 95 km H 6.0 ° N 109.2 ° E 50 km J 6.2 ° N 107.6 ° E 47 km K 4.6 ° N 107.6 ° E 26 km L 3.9 ° N 107.4 ° E 35 km M 3.1 ° N 107.0 ° E 18 km T 7.0 ° N 104.5 ° E 15 km
(src)="429221"> Visa requirements for Uzbekistani citizens are administrative entry restrictions by the authorities of other states placed on citizens of Uzbekistan .
(src)="429222"> As of 1 January 2017 , Uzbekistani citizens had visa-free or visa on arrival access to 53 countries and territories , ranking the Uzbekistani passport 83rd in terms of travel freedom ( tied with Ivorian , Senegalese , Tajik and Togolese passports ) according to the Henley visa restrictions index.[1 ] However , aside from foreign visa requirements , Uzbekistan is one of the few countries that imposes an exit visa regime on its citizens wishing to leave , and Uzbek citizens need an exit visa from their government for most international travel .
(trg)="1459"> O ‘ zbekiston Respublikasi fuqarolari uchun viza talablari  O ‘ zbekiston  fuqarolariga boshqa davlat fuqarolari tomonidan o ‘ rnatilgan ma ’ muriy kirish cheklovlaridir .
(trg)="1460"> 2017-yil  1-yanvar holatiga ko ‘ ra 53 ta davlat va hududlarga vizasiz kirish huquqiga egalar , O ‘ zbekiston fuqarolarning edi visa-bepul yoki visa bo ' yicha vorisi kirish uchun 53 mamlakatlar va hududlar , martabali Uzbekistani pasport 83rd jihatidan sayohat erkinlik ( bog ' lab bilan Ivorian , Senegalese , tojikiston va Togolese pasport ) ko ' ra Henley visa cheklovlar indeksi . [ 1 ] Ammo , chetga boshlab xorijiy viza talablari , O ' zbekiston bir necha mamlakatlar deb yuklaydi sababli bir chiqish viza rejimi uning fuqarolari istab uchun qoldiring , o ' zbek fuqarolari kerak , bir exit visa ularning hukumat uchun eng xalqaro sayohat .
(src)="429223"> All Uzbek citizens are required to obtain an exit visa to travel to all non-CIS countries .
(src)="429224"> An exit visa is not needed for a trip to a CIS country so long as the traveler does not then go to a non-CIS country .
(src)="429225"> Penalties for traveling to non-CIS countries without an exit visa include heavy fines and prison terms up to 10 years in length .
(src)="429226"> Exit visas are obtained from the Interior Ministry 's local OVIR ( Office of Visas and Registration ) , cost $25 , and are valid for two years .

(src)="429620"> Elon Reeve Musk ( /ˈiːlɒn ˈmʌsk/ ; born June 28 , 1971 ) is a South African-born Canadian-American business magnate , investor,[9][10 ] engineer,[11 ] and inventor.[12][13][14][15 ]
(trg)="1851"> Ilon Riv Mask ( / ˈiːlɒn ˈmʌsk / ; 28-iyun , 1971-yil Janubiy Afrikada tug ‘ ilgan ) Janubiy Afrika , Kanada va AQSH biznes magnati , investor , [ 9 ] [ 10 ] muhandis , [ 11 ] va ixtirochi . [ 12 ] [ 13 ] [ 14 ] [ 15 ]
(src)="429621"> He is the founder , CEO , and CTO of SpaceX ; co-founder , CEO , and product architect of Tesla Inc. ; founder and CEO of Neuralink ; co-founder and chairman of SolarCity ; co-chairman of OpenAI ; co-founder of Zip2 ; and founder of X.com , which merged with Confinity and took the name PayPal.[16][17][18][19 ] As of May 2017 , he has an estimated net worth of $15.2 billion , making him the 80th-wealthiest person in the world.[20 ] In December 2016 , Musk was ranked 21st on Forbes list of The World 's Most Powerful People.[21 ]

(src)="430151"> Recreation of Martin Luther King 's cell in Birmingham Jail at the National Civil Rights Museum
(trg)="2365"> Milliy Fuqarolik Huquqlari Muzeyida  Birmingham qamoqxonasidagi Martin Lyuter King kamerasining saqlanmasi
(src)="430152"> The Letter from Birmingham Jail , also known as the Letter from Birmingham City Jail and The Negro Is Your Brother , is an open letter written on April 16 , 1963 , by Martin Luther King Jr.
(src)="430153"> The letter defends the strategy of nonviolent resistance to racism .
(src)="430154"> It says that people have a moral responsibility to break unjust laws and to take direct action rather than waiting potentially forever for justice to come through the courts .
(src)="430155"> Responding to being referred to as an " outsider , " King writes , " Injustice anywhere is a threat to justice everywhere " .
(trg)="2366"> Birmingem Qamoxonasidan Noma , shuningdek  Birmingem Shahar Qamoqxonasidan Maktub  va Bu Habash Sizga Birodar  kabi nomlar bilan mashhur bo ' lib , 1963 yilning 16-aprelida Martin Luther King Jr .  ( Martin Lyuter King )  tomonidan yozilgan ochiq xat hisoblanadi .
(trg)="2367"> Ushbu xat irqchilikka qarshi kuch ishlatilmaydigan strategiyani himoya qiladi .
(trg)="2368"> Unda insonlarning adolatsiz qonunlarni buzishga va sudlarga adolat kelishini abadiy kutishning o ' rniga to ' g ' ridan-to ' g ' ri harakatlar qilish uchun axloqiy mas ' uliyatlari borligi aytiladi .
(trg)="2369"> Javob uchun bo ' lish ataladi kabi bir " begona , " Shoh yozadi , " Nohaqliklar har joyda bir tahdid uchun adliya hamma joyda " .
(src)="430156"> The letter , written during the 1963 Birmingham campaign , was widely published , and became an important text for the American Civil Rights Movement .
(trg)="2370"> 1963 yilgi  Birmingem kampaniyasida yozilgan ushbu maktub  keng nashr etilgan va  Amerika Fuqarolik Huquqlari Harakati  uchun muhim matnga aylandi .

(src)="430283"> Generative grammar is a linguistic theory that regards grammar as a system of rules that generates exactly those combinations of words that form grammatical sentences in a given language .
(src)="430284"> Noam Chomsky first used the term in relation to the theoretical linguistics of grammar that he developed in the late 1950s.[1 ] Linguists who follow the generative approach have been called generativists .
(src)="430285"> The generative school has focused on the study of syntax and addressed other aspects of a language 's structure , including morphology and phonology .
(trg)="2494"> Generativ grammatika ( ingliz . ʻʻgenerativeʼʼ - generativ , yaratuvchan , ʻʻgrammarʼʼ - grammatika ) - grammatikani maʼlum bir tilda soʻzlar birikmasi orqali tuzilish jihatidan toʻgʻri gaplar yaralishiga asos boʻluvchi qoidalar tizimi deb hisoblaydigan tilshunoslik nazariyasidir .
(trg)="2495"> Ushbu atamani birinchi boʻlib Noam Chomskiy 1950-yillarning oxirlarida oʻzi ishlab chiqqan tilshunoslik nazariyasiga tegishli qoʻllagan . [ 1 ] Generativ grammatika doirasida tadqiqot olib boruvchi tilshunoslar generativistlar deb nomlanadi .
(trg)="2496"> Generativ maktabi asosan sintaksis yoʻnalishi boʻyicha izlanishlar olib borishi bilan birga , tilshunoslikning boshqa yoʻnalishlari , xususan , morfologiya va fonetikaga ham eʼtibor qaratadi .
(src)="430286"> Early versions of Chomsky 's theory were called transformational grammar , a term still used to include his subsequent theories,[2 ] the most recent of which is the minimalist program theory : Chomsky and other generativists have argued that many of the properties of a generative grammar arise from a universal grammar that is innate to the human brain , rather than being learned from the environment ( see the poverty of the stimulus argument ) .
(trg)="2497"> Chomskiy nazariyasining dastlabki shakli transformatsion grammatika deb atalgan va bugungi kunda ushbu nazariyaning keyingi shakllarini [ 1 ] oʻz ichiga qamrab olgan , bularning eng soʻnggisi - minimalistik dastur .
(trg)="2498"> Chomskiy va boshqa generativistlarning fikriga ko ' ra , generativ grammatika xususiyatlari atrof-muhitdan oʻrganish evaziga emas , balki inson miyasidagi tugʻma universal grammatikadan kelib chiqadi .
(src)="430287"> There are a number of versions of generative grammar currently practiced within linguistics .
(trg)="2499"> Zamonaviy tilshunoslikda generativ grammatikaning turli tizimlari mavjud .
(src)="430288"> A contrasting approach is that of constraint-based grammars .
(src)="430289"> Where a generative grammar attempts to list all the rules that result in all well-formed sentences , constraint-based grammars allow anything that is not otherwise constrained .
(src)="430290"> Certain versions of dependency grammar , head-driven phrase structure grammar , lexical functional grammar , categorial grammar , relational grammar , link grammar , and tree-adjoining grammar are constraint-based grammars that have been proposed .
(src)="430291"> In stochastic grammar , grammatical correctness is taken as a probabilistic variable , rather than a discrete ( yes or no ) property .
